***alstublieft.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a> (455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:belieft.html>belieft</a></i>, literally "if it pleases you". Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">s'il vous plaît</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> please</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> here you are (when handing something to someone else)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>Alstublieft</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally used when giving a payment to a salesperson, to which the salesperson responds with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> or an equivalent. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used by the salesperson when returning change to the customer, in which case the customer responds with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> upon having received the change.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">a.<a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>.b.</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

***altaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:altaar.html>altaar</a> (7612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">altare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*altare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">altāre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alternator.html>alternator</a> (71216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">alternate</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-or</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:alternator.html>alternator</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">alternators</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An electric generator which produces alternating current through mechanical means.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:alternator.html>alternator</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(werktuigbouwkunde)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(elektrotechniek)</span> machine <a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mechanische.html>mechanische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:energie.html>energie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:binnenkomend.html>binnenkomend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:draaiende.html>draaiende</a> as, <a href = vnd.unilang:omgezet.html>omgezet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:elektrische.html>elektrische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wisselstroom.html>wisselstroom</a></li></ol>

***althans.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:althans.html>althans</a> (5115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thans.html>thans</a></i>. Originally, in the 17th century, it meant an emphatic version of “now”, as in “already now”, but this meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now outdated.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:althans.html>althans</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">at least</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> right now, now</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambacht.html>ambacht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambacht.html>ambacht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ambahtaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">ambaxtos</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*ambaxtos</i>. ***ambachtelijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ambachtelijk.html>ambachtelijk</a> (109736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambacht.html>ambacht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambachtelijk.html>ambachtelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ambachtelijker</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ambachtelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>artisanal; produced or producing <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the rules of traditional craft</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> exceedingly frequent in advertising in the Netherlands, particularly with foodstuffs. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not trademarked, however, and therefore largely meaningless.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ambachtelijk.html>ambachtelijk</a></b>

***ambassade.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ambassade.html>ambassade</a> (3811)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambassade.html>ambassade</a></i>, ultimately replacing <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ambassaat</i> as the general term.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambassade.html>ambassade</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambassades.html>ambassades</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambassade.html>ambassadetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An embassy, diplomatic legation to permanently represent a foreign state at (the highest) embassador's level.</li>
<li>An ambassadorial mission.</li>
<li>An embassy building.</li></ol>

***ambt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ambt.html>ambt</a> (13413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ampt</i>. Originally the same word as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambacht.html>ambacht</a></i> and possibly a mere variant of it. However, the fact that the earliest occurrences are found in texts by eastern writers, <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> it likely that this form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">ambet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambt.html>ambt</a></i> (whence modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Amt</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ambahti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ambahtaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">ambaxtos</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*ambaxtos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambt.html>ambt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambten.html>ambten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambt.html>ambtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>office, function, post <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an official position</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ambtelijk.html>ambtelijk</a> (119838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambt.html>ambt</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambtelijk.html>ambtelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ambtelijk.html>ambtelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ambtelijkst</b>)

<ol><li>official
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>Zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ambtelijk.html>ambtelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevel.html>bevel</a>.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Without an <b>official</b> order.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:amok.html>amok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:amok.html>amoks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A murderous frenzy, a killing spree in Malay culture.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:amok.html>amok</a>, someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on such a killing spree.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">amokmaker</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uproar, riot, noise</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:amok.html>amok</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***amper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a> (2327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inconclusive. Whilst its current definition <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> long thought to have come from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indonesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Indonesian language">Indonesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="id">hampir</i> due to its exclusive presence in Dutch (and no other Germanic language), this would not explain its high and almost universal usage in Flemish. More likely would be if it originated on Dutch soil. In that case, the meaning would have changed somewhat from the earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> – compare the semantic development of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sehr.html>sehr</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">very</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alemannic_German" class="extiw" title="w:Alemannic German">Alemannic German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gsw">rüüdig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">very</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This word, in turn, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Germanic, and a cognate to the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ampfer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>scarcely, barely
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeite.html>moeite</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waard.html>waard</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That's <b>barely</b> worth the effort!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nauwelijks.html>nauwelijks</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></strong>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sour</li></ol>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:amper.html>amper</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ademhalen.html>ademhalen</a>.</i> </li>

***ampul.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ampul.html>ampul</a> (19473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ampulle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ampule</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ampulla</i>, itself of unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ampul.html>ampul</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ampullen.html>ampullen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ampul.html>ampulletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An ampoule, small, closed (glass or artificial) vial, as used to dose medicine</li>
<li>A small jug, notably for liturgical use</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ampul.html>ampul</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:amputatie.html>amputatie</a> (30725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">amputation</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">amputātiō</i>. First attested in the sixteenth century.
</p>

</p>
